< review>
SUV overheated while parked and idling. Their shop was less than 3 miles away and AAA approved by Auto Club, which means service is warranteed. Although they were busy (towed on a Friday, returned on a Tuesday), the communication was stellar with respect to text message link to estimate, what to authorize, follow-up phone calls. Primary reason I gave 4 instead of 5 stars is that I felt labor was high to replace several hoses that blew plus a fee for subsequent check to ensure vehicle was working properly afterwards. It's the first time I've had radiator/HVAC hoses go out on any vehicle in well over 25+ years, so my surprise seeing close to $1k out the door was astonishing, let alone seeing the sadness and anger from my wife after telling her what the final cost was. Everyone we spoke with from arrival to pick up was wonderful and truly cares for the customer. Just trying to get past the pricing aspect.< /review>

<Review>NEEDS ZERO STARS.
They TOTALLED out my very rare truck!
More concerned about upselling then repairing!

LONG STORY BUT WORTH THE READ.
Took my 2008 King Ranch Expedition EL 4x4 for A/C recharge the summer before this incident to this shop and was told had a slow leak in the condenser but would probably make it through the summer with a freon recharge. At the end of the following summer I had enough with the A/C taking 30-45 minutes of highway driving for the air to get cold. The wife took the truck in and asked them to complete the repairs THEY had diagnosed from before. After also recommending a new radiator, that was very slowly leaking water from the seam, I agreed to the radiator as I was told the A/C condenser was indeed leaking freon and needed to be changed to fix the A/C. The tech and the desk lady both ensured the A/C would be fixed and a future water leak would also be averted; fine. After a week in the shop, I picked up the truck at 10am on a Friday (~80¬∞ outside) and the A/C temp felt exactly the same as it did the week before. Went right back to the shop and they confirmed the A/C system was full of freon BEFORE they started the work!... NOT leaking freon! Why then was $1,300+ of work and parts changed out and no proper diagnosis was made?! The leak they visually identified in the condenser was actually the Power Steering fluid collecting dirt through a very slow leak. Power steering lines run through the A/C condenser in many Fords and notoriously leak. The very rude tech, with metal @#&t hanging from his face, left a hose clamp for the transmission line off the new radiator. This cooked my transmission as I was driving later that day on the freeway when the hose blew off the fitting. The entire paint, underbody and engine bay was drenched in Transmission oil. Hydraulic oil is usually corrosive to paint. So AAA found that the Transmission got damaged when the oil drained out and the truck may possibly have electrical issues and need a new paint job in a few months if the clearcoat starts to peel. So they totalled it out. Left my family of 6 without a vehicle for six months until we could find an equivalent replacement that was CA smog legal. Thanks Auto DIAGNOSTICS for not actually diagnosing my A/C, it cost my family a truck that they all loved. Ended up with a totalled vehicle and A/C was never repaired properly by admission of the shop owner. Thankfully AAA and BofA are great and covered our loses. <Review>I lived at Parkway Lakes full time for almost 2 years. I was fortunate to be there after Don and Sharon took over. I can't begin to say enough about how well I was treated. It is a very quiet, shady, friendly place to call home. If you have ANY problem at all Don will make sure he attends to it right away. I am 75 years old and the only thing that was a problem for me there was having to carry my laundry to the washing facility. I solved that problem by buying a wheeled cart. I had two vehicles and was able to park both of them within my allowed space. Although I didn't attend all of them, Don and Sharon held a potluck every first Saturday of the month. They are very family oriented and it showed throughout the park. I was never bothered by noisy, bike riding children. In fact more times than not I was greeted in a very respectful manner by the children in the park. All in all I would say do not pass up the chance to stay here whether it is for an overnight, a week, a month or a year. I will never be sorry that I signed on with Don and Sharon. Thank you and your staff for a wonderful place to call home.</Review><date>1367342386972</date></record>

< Review>
Great selection. Comfy chairs. Excellent wifi. I come here to work remotely and smoke cigars and it is great.

Also they have some nice TVs to show sports. If you are a Bay Area team fan (Esp. Warriors, Raiders, and Giants) they show pretty much all the games and even generally stay open late till a game is over.

They also have humidor lockers to rent if you are into that.

It can be pretty cold inside. Bring a jacket.<//Review>
